#### Opcodes

```
  0: 0x02A3 [0x03] ExtData[1]->WorkLocal[0] = Work_Zone[2]
  1: 0x02A8 [0x03] ExtData[1]->WorkLocal[31] = Work_Zone[3]
  2: 0x02AD [0x03] ExtData[1]->WorkLocal[32] = Work_Zone[4]
```
